###Chapter 1 Pregnancy



"Sorry, the number you're trying to reach is unavailable right now..."



The robotic voice echoed again, but Yvonne Ellis didn't hang up right away. She sat at the long dining table with her phone pressed to her ear, calling Julian Powell,her husband,over and over, hoping he would answer just once.



Looking at the message she sent this morning-"It's our third wedding anniversary. Can you come home early?"-she sighed bitterly.


Julian had left her words unread, as if the date slipped from his mind.



But for Yvonne, it wasn't a shock. His heart had belonged to another woman for years, so how could he spare a thought for their marriage?


The truth was, Julian had only agreed to marry her to keep his grandfather, Rodger Powell, from worrying about him.



In the three years since, he had built walls around himself, refusing to talk to her and never even having sex with her. The clock struck twelve, and the candlelit dinner she had worked on for hours became a cruel joke.



She let out a shaky laugh, and tears ran freely down her cheeks. Lifting her glass, she emptied the wine in one swallow.



Alcohol was never her strength, and before long, the edges of her grief blurred into a light-headed daze.



She stumbled into the bedroom and collapsed onto the bed, her unfocused gaze fixed on the chandelier's bright glare.



Just as sleep threatened to pull her under, a warm touch brushed her collarbone, and she startled awake.Blinking rapidly, she found Julian seated at the edge of the bed.



His suit jacket was gone, his white shirt sleeves rolled up to his forearms. A gleaming watch caught the light as his wrist shifted. His long lashes lowered slightly,hiding the depth of his eyes. His expression was unreadable, his handsome features calm and distant.



Yvonne froze in shock for a brief moment before quickly sitting up. A rush of uncontrollable joy swept through her, and her voice quivered with excitement as she spoke. "You're finally home. Has it been a hectic day for you? Are you hungry? I can go make something for you right now..." Yvonne lurched out of bed in a panic, terrified he might walk away again. But her foot snagged the carpet,sending her straight into Julian's solid chest.The sharp bite of alcohol mixed with his familiar cologne wrapped around her like a warning.



The realization struck her all at once. He had been drinking heavily. That was the only reason he would be here, sitting on her bed when he normally kept his distance.



Even with his calm exterior, Yvonne knew better. His stiffness gave him away. Julian despised being touched by her, and his silence carried a weight she couldn't name.



She opened her mouth to speak, to apologize for the clumsy fall, but her eyes caught something that silenced her. A glaring lipstick stain bloomed against his collar. Her chest tightened, and a sharp ache tore through her.



"What's wrong?" His voice was low, almost gentle.


Snapping back, she pulled her hands away from his shoulders as if burned. "Sorry, I didn't mean to," she whispered, her apology tumbling out.


Before she could move farther, his palm pressed firmly against the back of her neck, holding her in place. His head dipped suddenly, and his lips crushed against hers.


Her eyes flew wide. The kiss was fierce and consuming,making her forget how to breathe.



Instinct told her to resist, and she pushed at his chest.However,his hold only grew stronger.


"I want you," he mumbled, the words rough and unsteady against her lips.



His other hand slipped beneath the hem of her satin nightdress, tracing the curve of her thigh with deliberate intent, climbing higher with each slow movement.



Heat rippled through her body, rising from her waist and surging up her spine until it clouded her thoughts.Rationality dissolved, leaving her lost in the pull of his touch.



For the first time in years, the hollow place inside her felt whole. And just before desire consumed her completely, one last clear thought flickered. Julian had to be heavily drunk-there was no other reason for this.







Sunlight slipped past the curtains when Yvonne finally opened her eyes, and the quiet rush of water from the bathroom told her Julian was awake before her. A dull ache spread through her body as she pushed herself upright, the blanket sliding down and baring the faint kiss marks along her collarbone-marks that felt surreal, considering how distant he had always been.


Her gaze drifted toward the closed bathroom door,her chest stirring with a confusing mix of disbelief and fragile hope.


He had finally chosen to have sex with her, and it left her wondering if this meant he was ready to open up to her, to put effort into understanding her and building their marriage.


That thought gave her strength to rise from the bed.She bent down to gather his discarded suit jacket,and from its pocket tumbled a bracelet that sparkled in the morning light.


The piece was breathtaking. A sapphire cut into the shape of a delicate flower gleamed at its center,ringed by sharp silver facets that caught the light like shards of ice.



As Yvonne traced its design with her fingers, the bathroom door opened. Julian stepped out, steam curling around him, a towel knotted low at his hips. His tall frame revealed sculpted lines, from the sharp cut of his abs to the deep V that led downward,every inch of him radiating effortless strength. His eyes flicked toward the bracelet in her hand. "It suits you," he said, his tone light, almost careless.



Her lips parted in surprise."Are you giving thisto me?"



Julian stopped abruptly on his track, studied her hopeful expression, then gave a brief nod. "Yes."Without another word, he crossed into the dressing room.



The coldness in his voice hit like a splash of icy water,making last night's closeness feel surreal, like it was merely a dream.



Yvonne watched his retreating back, a flicker of disappointment passing through her before she quickly steadied herself. She found comfort in knowing that their relationship was beginning to shift,and she held onto the belief that Julian would one day recognize her true value.



A small smile bloomed across her face as she admired the jewel in her palm. Maybe, just maybe, he was beginning to change.



From that day onward, she noticed the smallest shifts between them-quiet, subtle steps that hinted their marriage was no longer standing still. Dinner at the villa became less of a rarity, with Julian showing up at least twice a week now. The change in routine didn't go unnoticed. At a lavish afternoon tea, the wives of businessmen eyed Yvonne's brighter mood, their voices buzzing like bees.



One leaned forward with a smirk and asked, "Yvonne,something's different about you lately. You look radiant. What's the good news?"



Yvonne's lips curved in a modest smile, ready to share her newfound happiness, when a sudden wave of nausea surged. She bent forward, gagging, her reaction silencing the chatter around the table.



The startled looks that followed all said the same thing-the symptom wasn't foreign to these married women;was she pregnant?



The thought hit Yvonne with force. She remembered her missed cycle, her pulse quickening as disbelief clouded her mind.



She excused herself quickly, unable to sit there under the weight of their stares, and rushed straight to the hospital. Hours later, a crisp white envelope heldher answer.



"Eight weeks along. Congratulations," the doctor announced warmly. "You're going to be a mother."



The words barely sank in. Yvonne pressed her hand against her flat stomach, her eyes stinging with tears she hadn't expected.


Pregnancy had never crossed her mind, yet here it was staring her in the face.



The news left her reeling, and the first thought that followed was Julian. He would never celebrate this.His cutting words from the past echoed back-having a child with her was something humiliating.


A knot formed in her stomach. If he discovered the truth, he might demand she end it.


The thrill of the moment evaporated,leaving only dread. With a heavy sigh, she thanked the doctor politely and stepped out, her heart weighed down with uncertainty.


Still, she couldn't hide it forever. Whether he liked it or not, the child belonged to both of them, and Julian would eventually know.


Her hand shook as she scrolled through her contacts,searching for Julian's name. But a voice from a nearby exam room made her stop cold.



Through the doorway, she spotted Julian inside,steadying a striking woman onto a chair. The doctor's congratulatory words rang out.


"Mr.Powell, you're going to be a father. Your wife is eight weeks pregnant..."
###Chapter 2 Being Deceived



The sight of her husband accompanying another woman for a prenatal check-up hit Yvonne like a bomb going off inside her skull, leaving her dizzy and unsteady on her feet. And the shock rattled her,making her accidentally hit the dial button.



A few seconds later, Julian's voice drifted out from the exam room. "Hello?"



Yvonne kept her gaze locked on him through the half -open door, her throat tightening until her words shook hesitantly. "Where are you right now?"


Her mind spun in chaos. The doctor called that woman Julian's wife. Then what did that make her? Eight weeks ago lined up with the night he had sex with her for the first time. So, her husband had slept with another woman during the same week?



The weight of that thought nearly tore her apart.Tears blurred her vision as she squinted at the woman's face, and recognition struck like a blade.



Rita Adams. The name screamed inside her. The very woman who had lived in Julian's heart for years.


Yvonne remembered stumbling across Rita's picture in his study once, tucked away but cherished.


Stories about them had floated around too-how they had met overseas, how their shared passions had made them inseparable, how everyone had thought they were destined to be together. If not for her marriage to Julian, they would have been the couple people envied.


Only now did Yvonne grasp the truth. Rita had returned. And Julian had taken Rita back into his life.



It dawned on her with a cruel clarity-the wife he wanted had never been her. Her eyes filled until the tears slipped free, and the realization cut deep.



Had he already been with Rita before he had slept with her? The lipstick stain on his collar came rushing back to her memory. She finally understood. That trace must have belonged to Rita.


A heavy knot twisted in Yvonne's stomach, but hope,fragile and foolish, kept her eyes fixed on Julian's back, desperate for him to come clean.


Inside the room, his gaze flickered toward Rita before he answered, his tone smooth and detached, "I'm in a meeting at the office.Why are you calling?"


The lie cut through her like ice. For a moment her thoughts scattered, leaving only the burn of betrayal and rage. A bitter smile tugged at her lips, mocking herself for ever expecting honesty


There was no point in pressing further. Any question would only humiliate her more.


She ended the call without a word. Her body gave out as she slid down the cold wall, her hand clamping over her mouth to stifle the sobs that broke free.



A nurse passing by stopped, concern etched on her face."Are you all right?"


Meanwhile, something unsettled Julian. He turned his head slightly, as though sensing eyes on him, but the hallway beyond was empty. A faint frown creased his face.



Yvonne had never once defied him.For years she had bent quietly to his will, yet this time she had hung up before he even could. The abruptness gnawed at him.



An instinct urged him to leave and search for her. He stood up abruptly.



"Julian, who was it?" Rita's voice qquivered as she tugged on his sleeve, her delicate face tilted up in practiced vulnerability.


The moment broke, and Julian steadied himself. "Just work," he said evenly.


He eased his sleeve from her grasp, turned back to the doctor, and continued in that same calm voice,asking about the dos and don'ts during a pregnancy.



After Julian turned his focus back to the doctor, Rita's gentle mask slipped. Her eyes narrowed ever so slightly as she pulled out her phone beneath the table.Fingers moving quickly, she sent a message, saying,"I just spotted Yvonne at Kumvine Hospital. Check why she's seeing an OB-GYN."



Later, at the hospital entrance, Julian walked Rita to the car, his voice calm and detached. "Go home and get some rest."



Her hand froze on the door handle, and she turned back with a wounded look. "You're not coming with me? I don't want to be alone tonight... I'm scared."


His reply was immediate, smooth, and distant. "I've got things at the office that need attention."


Rita's fingers curled tightly against her palm, but within seconds she replaced the frustration with a sweet,understanding smile.I right. I'll wait for you at home."



Julian gave a short nod, watched the car roll away,and then headed for his own vehicle.



On the drive back, he dialed Yvonne's number again and again. Each time, the call rang unanswered until finally her phone switched off. By the time he sat at his desk, the weight in his chest had settled into something cold and heavy. His phone rested in his hand, his face shadowed by a stormy scowl.



Stacks of documents sat waiting, but the ink on the pages might as well have been invisible. His mind refused to focus.



The silence broke with Andrew Pearson, Julian's friend,barging into the office, grinning ear to ear. "Julian,congratulations! You're going to be a father!"



Julian's eyes darkened further, his jaw tightening Clearly Andrew must have caught wind of his accompanying Rita for a prenatal visit and jumped to conclusions. His voice came out sharp. "Stop spouting nonsense-"



But Andrew cut him off, too excited to notice the warning edge. "You really don't know yet? Yvonne was sick at a tea party today, looked just like morning sickness. Everyone's saying she's pregnant!"
###Chapter 3 His Choice



Yvonne dragged herself through the front door, her steps heavy as if every ounce of strength had been drained from her.


Kicking off her shoes, she stood still for a moment,her eyes roaming the dark, empty house. The corners of her lips curved into a hollow smile, one that carried no warmth.



Only now did she truly see how foolish she had been.This house had always been lifeless, just like Julian's heart. She had spent years guarding a place that was actually cold, silent, and meaningless,becoming little more than an object of pity.



It didn't surprise her that he wasn't home. He had spent the day at Rita's side, celebrating her pregnancy Most likely, he was still with her now, wrapped in tender moments that belonged only to them,imagining the family they would build together.



Every day before today, Yvonne would have already cooked a full dinner, set the table, and left the lights on,waiting for him with foolish hope.


But tonight, she didn't bother. She didn't even turn on the lights as she walked barefoot into the hollow living room, her body moving on autopilot.


When she reached the sofa, an unexpected hand shot out of the shadows, pulling her against a firm chest.



Her startled cry filled the room just as a lamp flickered on, bathing Julian's face in soft, golden light. His features looked carved from stone, flawless and distant.



Pressing a finger to her lips, he whispered, "It's me."


She froze, stunned by the sudden closeness. No matter how many times she told herself to stop caring,her heart still betrayed her, fluttering at the sight of him.



Julian let her go as quickly as he had pulled her in. The fleeting warmth vanished, leaving behind the same indifference as his voice turned cold, almost reproachful. "Where have you been all day? I tried calling you over and over, but you never answered."


Reality slammed back into her chest. The question was almost laughable. Shouldn't it be her demanding to know where he had spent his day?


She wanted to scream the truth at him, but the words never left her mouth. Instead, she curved her lips into a faint, steady smile and replied, "Yeah." Yeah? What was that supposed to mean? He was about to press further, but then he caught her eyes.


Something in her calm indifference made his irritation vanish. His words came out gentler, uncertain.'you all right? You look pale... are you sick?"


Yvonne dropped her gaze to the floor, realizing that the concern she once craved from him no longer carried the same weight.



Exhaustion pressed down on her, leaving no room to play the forgiving wife. Her voice was faint, almost detached. "I'm worn out. I need to rest."


She turned toward the stairs, but before she could take more than two steps, Julian's arm wrapped around her and pulled her back sharply against him.


Her body jolted from the force, and instinctively her hands flew to shield her stomach. Anger flared hot in her chest."What do you think you're doing?" she snapped.



Julian's eyes bore into her, his brow furrowing. "You're pregnant, aren't you?"


Her breath caught.He knew? But how?


A wild question flickered through her mind-if he had discovered her pregnancy, then would he choose her or would he still cling to Rita? "I..." The admission trembled on her lips, but the sudden shrill ring of his phone sliced through the moment.



Julian picked up his phone and answered the call.A soft, tearful voice came through the receiver,trembling with pain. "Jules, I slipped in the bathroom,and my stomach hurts so badly. Can you come over?The baby..."


Julian's face hardened instantly, urgency sharpening his tone. "Don't move. I'm on my way right now."


The call ended, and without hesitation he shoved Yvonne aside, striding toward the door with long,determined steps.



Her vision blurred as tears welled, the sting cutting deep. One plea from Rita, and he could abandon her without a backward glance.



Bitterness unlike anything she had felt before clawed up her throat. For once, she wanted to force the truth out of him, to know where his loyalty lay-was it ever with her, or had it always been with Rita?



She rushed forward, fingers clutching his sleeve desperately. Her lips parted, but before she could beg him to stay, his voice snapped like a whip. "Whatever it is, save it until I get back!" Her restraint shattered. Her voice shook violently as she cried out, "Where are you going? Who was that woman? You're my husband, Julian. How can you..."


The words she wanted to hurl at him caught in her throat. In that instant, it struck her-maybe she had been wrong all along.



Two months of routine dinners and fleeting gestures had tricked her into believing in something that was never real. She had let herself dream of a marriage that only existed in her imagination, forgetting that Julian had never once offered his heart.



Their marriage had always been a transaction,nothing more than a carefully staged illusion.



Julian's hand moved with a cold precision as he pried her fingers away from his sleeve. His eyes, sharp and merciless,pinned her down like a blade. "Yvonne, stop deceiving yourself. I told you from the start-I don't love you. Whatever I do is none of your concern."



Her heart hollowed at the cruelty in his tone. Her chest tightened painfully at his bluntness. She loosened her hold, a broken sob slipping past her lips as she whispered, "I'm sorry... I went too far..."


Julian lingered only long enough to cast her a silent,cutting look. Without another word, he turned and walked out, the door slamming behind him with finality.


The echo of that sound told her everything-whatever fragile tie had existed between them had just snapped.


Julian's chilling stare refused to leave her thoughts,replaying like a cruel reminder she couldn't escape.


Her stomach twisted, and she stumbled toward the bathroom, hand pressed over her mouth until she collapsed in front of the toilet.


Nothing but water spilled out-she had eaten almost nothing all day, yet her body convulsed as though punishing her further.


The spasms wracked her frame, and tears blurred her vision. With trembling fingers, she rested her palm against her flat belly, a broken laugh escaping through the pain. "Little one, you couldn't have chosen a worse moment to arrive. I'm the only person in this world who wants you."
###Chapter 4 Pretense



Julian never returned that night,leaving Yvonne sitting on the bathroom floor with her back pressed to the cold wall, her eyes wide open until morning crept in.


When dawn broke, the haze in her vision slowly cleared. She pushed her head up with effort, every muscle stiff and uncooperative. A sharp ache twisted in her abdomen, and even breathing felt heavy.



An endless night of wrestling with her thoughts had carved one truth into her heart-Julian didn't care for her. Clinging to him would only destroy her spirit and endanger the child within her.



If he despised the baby, then she would love it all the more.



Clutching the toilet for balance, Yvonne forced herself to stand. She staggered out of the bathroom and asked a servant to cook her something ligght.


The staff knew better than to meddle. They had long understood the strained bond between their employers and stayed silent.


On the sofa, Yvonne spooned porridge into her mouth,and with each swallow, a bit of warmth trickled back  into her frail body.


Her moment of peace ended when Sebastian Price,the butler, entered with two servants hefting a large canvas.



He bowed politely. "Mrs. Powell, this is the painting Mr.Powell commissioned for his grandfather's birthday.Will you and Mr. Powell be attending the celebration together?"



Her heart stuttered as the date struck her-Rodger's birthday. The marriage contract demanded she and Julian appear inseparable and they visit Rodger during holidays and family occasions, especially on this day.


But after the bitterness of last night, shecouldn't imagine standing beside Julian and pretending.



Even so, Yvonne had no escape. She sent a message with trembling fingers, saying, "Will you be going with me to the Powell Mansion for Rodger's birthday?"


No reply came. Her chest tightened as she forced herself to call him. The phone rang, then fell silent,unanswered.



Maybe he was still in Rita's bed, too exhausted to pick up.


For a split second, Yvonne's mind emptied, leaving her frozen in place. She forced her lips into a faint smile as she said, "I'll head over ahead of him."



Sebastian gave a slight bow, his calm expression hinting that he had already expected her answer.



Choosing not to dwell on it, Yvonne retreated to her room. The mirror reflected a face drained by a sleepless night, shadows etched beneath her eyes.She painted on foundation layer by layer,trying to hide what rest had failed to restore.



By the time she walked outside, the familiar car slid through the gates. The window lowered, and one detail struck her instantly-Julian wore clothes he hadn't left the house in the night before.


Her lashes lowered as her hands curled tight, digging crescents into her palms.



The truth was plain. He had spent the night with Rita,even taking the time to change into something from her place.



Julian's voice broke through her thoughts. "Get in."



Her teeth caught her lower lip before she responded,"Sebastian can drive me."



He shot her a piercing glance, his voice cold and cutting. "Do you really want Grandfather to notice any trouble between us?" The words lodged in her throat. With no choice, she opened the door and sat stiffly beside him.


Silence pressed down inside the car, neither willing to speak first.



A sidelong glance at him made her stomach twist. His clothes, his uncharacteristic casualness, all carried Rita's fingerprints.



The thought sickened her. Her chest heaved, and suddenly she gagged.



Julian's brows drew together as he turned toward her,startled, but before he could ask anything,Yvonne snapped her gaze away and stared coldly out the window.



She decided to match his silence, giving him the very treatment he had so often used on her.



The drive crawled by without a single word spoken between them.



When the car rolled to a stop at the Powell Mansion's gates, she unfastened her seatbelt before it fully braked and got out, striding forward with quick steps.


Julian caught up in only a few strides, his hand closing firmly around hers. Irritation sharpened his voice."Enough of this. Do you want Grandfather to see us at odds and expect me to bend to you?"


She inhaled deeply,shoving down her disappointment until only a brittle smile remained. "Relax. I'll play the role. Rodger won't suspect a thing."


His lips flattened into a thin, unyielding line. After a tense pause, he murmured indifferently, "You'd better mean that."



The coldness in his tone hollowed her out.Memories of nights spent yearning for him blurred her eyes with unshed tears, but she clung to one fragile hope."Then promise me something in return."



His brow creased, and her fists tightened until her nails bit her skin. Keeping her voice steady,she added,"Cut ties with her. If we're going to act like an inseparable couple, we can't let whispers of your affair reach the family. It'll ruin everything."



Even as the plea left her lips, she hated how small it made her sound. Still, some stubborn corner of her heart wanted to salvage their broken marriage.


To Julian, it was nothing but another unreasonable demand. He gave a sharp,mocking laugh, preparing to bite back.



Before he could, a firm voice, aged yet commanding,drifted from inside the mansion. "And what is it y/Ou two are discussing?” Rodger sat in his wheelchair, which was wheeled by Jordy Powell, Julian's father.
###Chapter 5 Morning Sickness
 The sudden appearance of Rodger and Jordy shattered the intense disagreement that had settled between Julian and Yvonne.



Julian's expression shifted in an instant, his lips curving into a warm smile as he slipped an arm around Yvonne's shoulders.


"Grandpa," he said smoothly, voice laced with forced calm, "Yvonne's upset because she thinks the gift l chose isn't impressive enough."



While the words flowed easily from his mouth, his eyes flicked toward her with a sharp, unspoken warning.



Yvonne almost laughed at the sheer artistry of his performance. Compared to him,she felt like a clumsy novice, managing only a stiff smile and a small nod.


Rodger's booming laughter filled the air, his gaze twinkling with teasing warmth as it landed on her."What more could I ask for than seeing the two of you so harmonious? But if you really want to give me the best gift, then bring me a strong great-grandchild soon." Without meaning to, Yvonne's hand drifted to her stomach, her eyes lowering as a shadow of sorrow crossed her face.



She carried that very child inside her, yet deep down she doubted Julian wanted it to exist.



Noticing the shift in her expression, Julian quickly interjected, eager to steer the moment away. "Let's not linger here. Everyone must be waiting inside."



The group moved into the lavishly adorned living room,where the younger generation of the Powell family had already gathered.


As they entered, Nadine Powell, Julian's aunt, glided forward with a warm smile, slipping her hand into Yvonne's and looking her over with concern. "How are you holding up, dear? You look thinner than before.Has Julian been considerate enough?"



Julian, standing just behind, looped an arm around Yvonne's waist and replied with mock indignation,"Aunt Nadine,how could I ever fail to take care of her?"



Though Yvonne recognized it for the empty act it was,her chest gave a faint flutter. She tilted her head upward just as he looked down, and for the briefest second, something softer seemed to linger in his eyes



Right then, a gentle voice drifted in fromn the doorway. "Julian."



Every head in the room turned, revealing Rita standing meekly just behind Sharon Powell, Julian's mother.


The atmosphere thickened at once, the cheerful chatter collapsing into uneasy silence.


Rodger's expression hardened, his eyes narrowing on Sharon.His voice thundered across the room. "This is a family gathering. Why would you bring an outsider here?"



Caught off guard, Sharon's cheeks flushed with embarrassment. "I only ran into Rita during a yoga class. She said she wanted to offer you birthday wishes..."



Rodger cut her off with a sharp glare. "I don't need empty greetings from a shallow woman like her,who only chases after wealth. Have you all forgotten the disgrace she caused us back then?"



No one dared answer. The Powells exchanged silent,knowing looks. Yvonne alone stayed bewildered,her thoughts racíng.



What disgrace? What had happened back then?Wasn't it Rodger who had pushed Julian into marrying her in the first place?



Sharon's eyes flicked briefly toward Yvonne but  quickly turned away. Her tone softened as she said,"There was a misunderstanding before. And Rita didn't just come to offer her wishes. She's a close friend of Dr. Jarrod Carter, the renowned heart surgeon. His team has been working on a new specialty medicine that could ease your chronic heart ailment."



At those words, Nadine's and Jordy's faces changed in an instant. Their cool disdain melted into eager anticipation as their gazes fixed on Rita. Even Julian's guarded expression faltered, surprise flashing across his eyes as he looked at her.


Rodger's failing heart had long weighed over the family, a shadow no physician had managed to lift.Age only worsened the condition, stealing his strength and leaving the Powells anxious with every passing year.



For them, the promise of a new specialty medicine was more precious than gold. If it truly existed, they would pay any price to secure it.


At once, the family crowded around Rita, hope flickering in their eyes.


Julian stepped forward, his voice urgent. "Rita, how do you know Dr. Carter? Can this specialty medicine really work for my grandpa?"


Encircled by the crowd, Rita gave a timid smile and answered in a gentle voice, which only deepened Yvonne's sense of being alone and set apart from everyone else.



Her teeth pressed into her lip as she watched. To Yvonne, it felt like Rita was the one who truly belonged, while her own place in the Powell family existed only because she carried the title of Julian's wife.



The idea haunted her. If they ever discovered Rita was carrying Julian's child, she was certain the family would welcome Rita far more than her.



Rodger,however, wasn't swayed by talk of medicine or promises of cures. Instead, his expression darkened,and he struck the armrest of his wheelchair with a sharp smack to silence the room.


Fixing Rita with a stern glare, Rodger asked, "Tell me,what is your real reason for coming back this time?"



Rita flinched at his words, clutching at Julian's sleeve as tears brimmed in her eyes. "Rodger, I only wanted to see Julian again. I don't have any other motives..."


Julían placed a hand on her shoulder, his voice gentling as he leaned in to comfort her.


The sight made Yvonne's stomach twist. She clamped a hand over her mouth and stumbled out of the room,rushing to the bathroom to vomit. The Powell family was caught off guard, and Nadine leaned in to whisper softly, "Yvonne's condition looks like the early signs of pregnancy, like morning sickness."



Julian's eyes narrowed at once, his expression unreadable as a storm of thoughts crossed his mind.
###Chapter 6 Confirmation



Yvonne felt weak after retching, her knees still trembling as she lifted her gaze to the mirror.The pale,worn-out facestaring back at her made her chest tighten. With a heavy sigh, she splashed cold water over her face, then dabbed on a quick layer of makeup to cover the fatigue before stepping out.



The last thing she expected was Julian waiting at the door. He stood against the wall with a lazy elegance,arms folded, one leg crossed over the other, as though he had been there all along. A knot of unease tightened in her chest.



Before she could decide what to say, he held out a crisp handkerchief,its faint scent startlingly fresh.



Caught off guard, she took it hesitantly. "Thanks."


Julian's eyes, dark and unreadable, fixed on her. you sick? I heard you were nauseous during the gathering yesterday too. I've already arranged for you to see a doctor this afternoon."



Her breath faltered. She wanted to refuse,but his tone left no room for choice-it wasn't a suggestion but a command. Without waiting for her response, he turned and walked away,leaving her rooted to the spot, her mind spinning.



Now was the worst possible time to reveal her pregnancy. Julian already had Rita carrying his child,and with the family's affection leaning toward that woman, she was certain he would choose Rita over her.



Drifting through a haze of worry, Yvonne slipped out of the bathroom and wandered down the hallway. Her steps slowed as voices of Jordy and Sharon floated from the study, tension sharp enough to stop her in her tracks.



She hadn't meant to eavesdrop, but Jordy's frustration echoed into the hall,impossible to ignore.



"Why bring Rita here of all days? Are you trying to humiliate Yvonne on purpose?" asked Jordy.



Sharon sounded close to tears, her voice brittle. "Do you honestly think I wanted this? Rita confided in me -she's expecting."



A heavy silence followed. When Jordy finally spoke,his disbelief was clear. "Are you telling me Julian's the father?"



Sharon's voice dropped to a hush, yet every word was edged with certainty. "Julian took her to the hospital just days ago. If the child isn't his, why would he go to such lengths?"



A weary sigh slipped from Jordy. "I never imagined Julian and Rita would cross paths again, let alone reconcile. And there is Yvonne-I feel pity for her."



Sharon's answer came without hesitation. "Whether we like it or not, Rita carries Julian's child. He never cared for Yvonne, and I doubt he'd want a child with her. This baby must be protected."



Jordy's tone hardened, leaving no room for debate."Yvonne can't know. If she finds out now,it will only humiliate her further."



What neither of them realized was that Yvonne had already heard enough.



Frozen at the study door, she felt her heart cave in at the confirmation that Rita was indeed carrying Julian's child.



Terrified they might notice her, she scrubbed the tears from her cheeks and fled down the hall, her chest tight with grief.



By the time she composed herself and rejoined the others in the living room, Jordy and Sharon had returned as well. Conversations halted, and all eyes landed on her, the air thick with awkward unease. Rodger's face creased with concern as he asked gently,"Yvonne, you don't look well. Should I call my physician to check on you?"



She forced a quick shake of her head. "There's no need, Rodger. The change in weather has just upset my stomach a little."



Rita lingered nearby, her gaze sharp. A fleeting, cold smile flickered at her lips. She had done her investigation and uncovered the truth-Yvonne was pregnant. It was news she swore the Powell family could never be allowed to discover.



Her return carried only one goal-to take Yvonne's place and become Julian's wife, no matter the cost.



With Yvonne hiding her pregnancy, she would be a fool not to exploit the opportunity.


That thought in mind, she slipped a small bottle of pills from her handbag, arranging her features into gentle concern. She stepped toward Yvonne and said sweetly, "Yvonne, you should try this if you're not feeling well. Dr. Carter's team created it. I used to struggle with stomach issues, but ever since I started on this, I've barely felt sick at all."


Sharon's lips curved into a smile as she added warmly,"If Dr. Carter's team developed it, then it must be reliable." Rita's eyes widened innocently, though her voice carried a subtle edge. "There's just one thing-it's not safe for expectant mothers. It can cause miscarriages.But of course, you can take it, Yvonne... you're not pregnant,right?"



The room fell into silence as every gaze shifted to Yvonne. In one breath, Rita had cornered her completely.



Yvonne's fingers curled into her palm, hidden from view, though her lips lifted in a calm smile as she accepted the bottle. "Thank you, Rita. I'll take it later."


Rita urged, "You shouldn't wait-take it now, and you won't have any stomach pain later. Let me fetch you some water." She hurried to pour a glass and placed it before Yvonne with exaggerated care.



To the family, Rita's actions looked full of kindness.But to Yvonne, Rita's eyes told a different story-sharp with challenge, glinting with malice.


Yvonne narrowed her gaze slightly, though her lips curving upward. "Alright then, I'll take it now."


Under the weight of everyone's stares, she slipped a pill into her hand and lifted it toward her mouth.
###Chapter 7 Flee


Yvonne's every move had Rita practically buzzing with anticipation. She wished more than anything to force that pill into Yvonne's mouth herself.



If Yvonne lost the baby, she'd no longer be a problem.


Right before the pill reached Yvonne's lips, a hand shot out and seized her wrist.



Yvonne jumped, glancing over to find Julian standing there,his face unreadable. He gave her wrist a steady shake until the pill tumbled from her grasp and hit the floor.



Turning to Rita, Julian said without much emotion, "I'LL take her to the hospital and get things checked out.She shouldn't take any medicine until we know exactly what's happening."



Annoyance flashed across Rita's features, though she managed to plaster on a gentle smile. "Of course,you're right. It's safer that way."



While Yvonne traced her wrist where Julian had touched her, warmth still lingering, her feelings twisted up inside. Maybe he was worried about her. The idea barely had time to settle before she brushed it away, a bitter little smile on her lips. Why let herself get fooled again?Most likely, Julian just wanted to put on a show for Rodger.


With a shake of her head, she forced herself to let it go, not realizing that Julian's gaze lingered on her for a long moment.



Trying to lighten the mood, Sharon suggested they all sit down for lunch.



Sharing a table with Rita left Yvonne with no appetite.An uncomfortable heaviness settled over the meal,making the atmosphere feel stifling.



As soon as she could, Yvonne rose from her seat,snatched up her bag, and turned to Rodger to say goodbye.



Rodger raised his gaze, his tone full of concern as he glanced at Julian, who was still deep in conversation with Rita. "Are you planning to visit the hospital by yourself? Wasn't Julian supposed to go with you?"



Swallowing her annoyance, Yvonne decided not to call Julían out. She offered a patient reply."Of course Julian's coming with me."


 
She then called over to him, making sure her words carried. "Honey, it's time to head to the hospital."


Hearing her call him "honey," Julian grew noticeably tense.Even knowing she was only acting, he still felt his heart skip a beat.


He walked away from Rita and approached Yvonne,picking up her bag as if it were the most natural thing in the world. "Come on, let's get going," he said,his tone gentle.


As they bid farewell to the Powell family and walked toward the door, they appeared the picture of a devoted couple.



Strolling through the garden, they heard hurried footsteps behind them.



Rita caught up, her face drained of color as she quietly pleaded with Julian, "Julian, I don't feel well. Can you drop me home first? I really don't want to go to the hospital."



Julian's eyes shifted to Yvonne, clearly torn. After a moment, he spoke up. "I'll have the driver take you to the hospital, Yvonne. I need to get Rita home first."


Yvonne had expected this, but it still stung. She forced a casual smile. "Go on.It's fine."



Wasting no more time, Julian turned to walk away with Rita. Left standing by herself, Yvonne fought back tears.She blinked fast, but the tears spilled over anyway.


Trying to stay positive, she reminded herself that at least there would be no need to come up with lies about her pregnancy.


Choosing some solitude, she set off for home on foot,hoping the walk would help her settle down.


As she was leaving the neighborhood, her phone vibrated. An unknown number had sent her a video,the preview showing Julian's familiar profile behind the wheel.



Confused,she opened the message and tapped on the video. The clip began with Julian driving, while Rita's voice floated in from the side.



"Julian, what if Yvonne really is pregnant? Would you take responsibility for the child?"



That question made Yvonne freeze. She paused the video, her heart beating fast. Her finger hovered over the screen, torn between curiosity and dread.


Did Julian truly want her to have the baby? She found herself needing to know.



Taking a steadying breath, she hit play once more.
###Chapter 8 Suffocating Ache
The video rolled on, every frame heavy with inevitability.


Julian's voice rang out, cool and detached,like a final judgment handed down from on high. "We were never going to have children."


After a brief pause, his words landed like a blade,driving straight at Yvonne through the screen. "Even if she were expecting, I would arrange for her to abort.Our marriage is nothing but a contract."


Yvonne's hand quivered, her knuckles pale from the force of her grip. The phone slipped through her trembling fingers and clattered against the ground with a sharp crack.



She had braced herself for cruelty, had rehearsed hearing the worst-but the unfeeling finality in Julian's voice still hollowed her out, leaving her chest tight and her breath shallow as the truth carved straight through her defenses.



The video still hadn't ended. Rita's syrupy voice cut through the silence like a whip across Yvonne's skin."What about the child I'm carrying?" Yvonne's chest constricted. Against her will, her eyes darted toward the phone lying on the ground, as if she could drag the answer out with sheer desperation.


A suffocating silence stretched on in the video. From the camera's angle, Julian's face remained hidden, his expression unreadable, his thoughts locked away.



"I'll take care of you and the child." His reply came at last-brief, unyielding, and mercilessly decisive.


Hot tears flooded Yvonne's eyes. Yet, almost punishing herself, she kept replaying the video, again and again, as though repeated exposure might somehow dull the sting of his heartlessness.



But she had overestimated her strength. Each replay carved deeper into her chest, until the agony dulled into a hollow numbness.



Without warning, Yvonne clutched her chest and gasped, her body collapsing against a cold roadside pillar.



The suffocating ache was no longer a metaphor-it was terrifyingly real. Her breaths came short and shallow,each one harder to draw.



Then a stabbing pain twisted through her abdomen,and dread surged instantly. Cold sweat streamed down her pale face. Gripping the pillar for balance, she slid into a crouch,her whole body trembling with fear.



Her eyes burned as tears blurred her vision, and she groped for the fallen phone on the ground. When the screen lit up, her finger hovered over one name, then stilled.



She asked herself whether she needed to call Julian.No-he could never learn about the baby.



She bit her lower lip hard, then scrolled and tapped another contact.



The line connected almost instantly, and a gentle male voice, laced with a touch of surprise, filled her ear. "Hello? Yvonne? Why are you calling me out of the blue? Did something happen?"



"L..." Yvonne opened her mouth, but before words could form, a sudden dampness spread beneath her.Glancing down, she froze in horror at the sight of blood pooling faintly onto the ground.


Her mind went blank. Trembling, she choked out."Spencer...I-I think I'm losing my baby!"







At Kumvine Medical Center, a man in a crisp white coat stood at the bedside. His tall frame and long legs lent him an imposing presence, his sculpted features almost too perfect, like a portrait brought to life. Yet the hard line of his brows carried the sharp, unyielding weight of authority.



Spencer Briggs's voice cut through the sterile room,deep and severe. "If I had been even a little later,you wouldn't have been able to keep this baby."


Lowering her gaze, Yvonne sat quietly, shoulders hunched like a reprimanded student enduring a lecture.Whenever Spencer spoke in that clipped,scolding tone, it meant he was truly furious.


And she couldn't blame him. Dragging a world-renowned neurosurgeon away from his work only to make him act as her obstetrician-anyone would find that infuriating.



Spencer drew in a steady breath, forcing down the edge in his voice. When he spoke again,it carried a gentler warmth. "Your pregnancy is fragile right noW.You need to stay calm, rest properly, and avoid stress.Do you understand?"


"| will," Yvonne answered softly, her gaze lifting to meet his. A faint shimmer lingered in her eyes."Spencer... thank you."


The gratitude in her voice was quiet but genuine, carrying the weight of her heart.


Spencer and Yvonne had grown up side by side,inseparable as children. Yet after Yvonne's marriage to Julian, she slowly pulled away from her crcle,letting every old friendship fade.


Spencer remained the rare exception. Even after years of distance, one call from her was enough to bring him running, and she silently vowed to hold this friendship close.


When Spencer's gaze met hers, the warmth in his eyes was shadowed by a storm of unspoken feelings.After wrestling with the thought, he finally asked,his voice low, "Why isn't Julian here with you?"


The question carved through her like a blade.Yvonne's chest tightened,her weary eyes fixed on the emptiness before her. With a heaviness that seemed to drain the very air around her, she murmured, "I'm going to divorce him."
###Chapter 9 Message



The steady rush of water from the bathroom in Rita's apartment stirred a flood of suggestive thoughts.



Standing by the doorway, Rita held out a set of men's pajamas, her cheeks tinged pink as she gave a timid knock. "Julian, I brought you something to wear."


There was a short pause before Julian answered from within, his tone distant, "Just leave them outside the door."



Hearing that, Rita's smile faded, and disappointment flashed in her eyes. She glanced down at the pile of Julian's clothes, carelessly dropped by the bathroom entrance.



His expensive gray suit was marked by a large coffee stain, and his phone had slipped out of the pocket.


A spark of intrigue lit up Rita's eyes. At that moment,the phone buzzed and the screen illuminated. It was a message from Yvonne.


Her pulse quickened as she cast a glance at the bathroom. Moving with care, she reached for his phone. The screen displayed Yvonne's message. "Will you be home tonight? I need to talk to you about something."


To Rita,it was obvious what Yvonne was after; she scoffed at Yvonne's scheme, sure that Yvonne only wanted to lure Julian back to her side.



A faint, mocking laugh slipped from Rita at the thought. She entered the password she'd memorized after casually noticing it a few times when Julian wasn't careful.



Still on edge, afraid Julian might appear at any second,Rita decided not to linger. She hurried to open Yvonne's chat and typed. "I'm busy right now. Don't message me."


She sent the message with a hint of satisfaction,quickly erasing the chat history afterward. Just as she moved to slip the phone back into Julian's suit pocket,the bathroom door suddenly opened


Julian stepped out, catching her red-handed, still holding his phone.


Rita stood there, frozen in place, comforted only by the fact that she'd already wiped the conversation.


He stared at the phone in her hand, a deep frown settling on his face. "What are you doing with that?" Rita avoided his gaze, but her movements were swift as she passed the phone back with a look of feigned innocence. "It slipped to the floor, so I picked it up for you."



Julian accepted the phone and went straight to the chat with Yvonne. The most recent message was his own, asking if she had reached the hospital, but she hadn't responded. Growing annoyed, he locked the phone.



Rita,still wearing a wounded look, handed over the pajamas. "I'm really sorry, Julian. I was so careless with the coffee.Please change into these."



Wrapped in nothing but a towel, Julian's broad shoulders and toned physique caught Rita's hungry stare.



Back when she'd let him go, she never imagined she'd regret it, but seeing him now, successful and striking,she refused to lose her chance again.



While Julian looked at the pajamas, his thoughts drifted. He remembered the way Yvonne's eyes lingered on him when he'd worn something out of his character that morning.



A strange question popped up-was Yvonne feeling jealous? On a sudden whim, Julian reached for his coffee-stained suit and pulled it back on. He looked at Rita and spoke flatly. "Don't worry about it. Since you're fine, I'm heading home."



Rita's hopeful smile faded in an instant. In desperation,she wrapped her arms around his waist. "It's already so late. Can't you stay with me?"



He gave her a stern look, then pulled her hands away with no hesitation. "You've gone too far, Rita."



Frozen in disbelief, Rita could only watch as Julian left the apartment without so much as a glance back.Resentment slowly twisted across her face.


Back when they were still a couple, Julian would never walk away from her like this. Now, though, his patience had clearly run out.


In her mind, all of this was Yvonne's fault.



Moving to the window, Rita stared at Julian's car pulling away, a wicked smile curling her lips. "I underestimated you, Yvonne. But don't get too comfortable. Sooner or later, Julian will be mine,and only mine."
###Chapter 10 Blocked



Julian entered the villa, finding nothing but darkness waiting for him. A frown creased his brow as he flicked on the lights. By habit, he reached behind to hand off his suit jacket, only to realize that nobody was there to take it. The empty hallway made him pause, leaving him momentarily thrown off.



Back then, opening this door always revealed Yvonne waiting beneath the warm light, smiling as she came forward to take his suit jacket and coax him toward dinner.



Tonight, the dining table stood bare, and not a soul waited nearby.



A tight line formed on his lips, irritation rising as he wondered why she still hadn't come back.


The noise awakened the housekeeper, Paula Tucker,and she rushed out to see what was happening.



Spotting Julian,she froze for a brief moment before awkwardly taking the suit jacket from his hands. "Mr.Powell, I'm so sorry. We assumed you wouldn't be coming back tonight, so we turned in early..."


Watching Paula struggle with his jacket, Julian couldn't help but think how differently Yvonne would have handled it, always smoothing out every crease.The small detail only soured his mood further.



He cut to the point. "Where's Yvonne? Hasn't Sebastian taken her back from the hospital?"



After a brief pause, Paula spoke up truthfully."Sebastian didn't take Mrs. Powell to the hospital today. She said she could manage on her own and told him to return ahead of her."



The chill in Julian's voice was unmistakable. "She went by herself? Where is she now?"



Paula, flustered, spoke with extra care. "She hasn't come home at all tonight. She called to leave a few instructions... She mentioned she won't be back until you give her an answer about that issue."


That answer caught Julian off guard. "What issue?"


Paula gave a small, puzzled shake of her head, which only deepened Julian's confusion. Pulling out his phone, he typed a message to Yvonne. "Where are you?"



His screen flashed with a red exclamation mark; he had been blocked. The realization left him speechless.


Paula caught sight of his screen and gasped, eyes wide.Yvonne, the woman who had once loved Julian so deeply, had actually blocked him? What could have possibly led to this?


Julian felt Paula's eyes on him, and fury surged through him. He slammed his phone onto the table,then snatched it back, frustration simmering. Without thinking, he searched his contacts and tried calling Yvonne.



The call didn't go through; she had also blocked his number, just as he'd feared. His expression turned even colder.



Paula stood there, shrinking under the tension, eyes downcast.



All at once, Julian spun sharply and headed for the door.



Holding his suit jacket close, Paula hesitated before softly asking, "Mr. Powell, should I have this sent to the cleaners?"



Yvonne used to handle every detail for Julian, so the staff rarely knew what to do on their own.


He stopped in his tracks, irritation lacing his words."Just throw it away."


As Paula started to obey, Julian spun around and walked back to her, his face unreadable. "Hand me your phone." No amount of reasoning could make him accept that Yvonne had really blocked him. He was set on finding out exactly why.



Paula faltered for a moment before gathering the nerve to speak. "Did you and Mrs. Powell have an argument? Maybe a calm conversation can help smooth things..."


A memory of their last argument flashed in Julian's mind. At the time, he'd brushed off Yvonne's concerns,thinking she was making a fuss over nothing.In hindsight, everything had shifted after that night.


Yvonne had pulled away, leaving him uneasy, as if he was losing control over something important.


Maybe he should never have picked that fight with her that night.


He couldn't shake the regret, though his face stayed hard. "Your phone, Paula."



Paula didn't say another word as she handed her phone to him, nerves making her hands shake.



Without a pause, Julian keyed in Yvonne's number smoothly and waited for the call to go through.



The call was answered almost instantly this time, and Yvonne's soft voice came through. "Hello? Paula?" Julian tightened his lips before answering in a low,steady tone, "It's me."
###Chapter 11 Divorce Agreement
A heavy silence hung in the air after Julian spoke.When Yvonne finally replied, her voice had lost all warmth."Anything?"



Hearing that,Julian's frown deepened. He wasn't used to her icy tone and responded with even less emotion,"Tell me where you are."



"It doesn't concern you. I'm busy, and I'd rather not be bothered," Yvonne said,her reply sharp. She ended the call before he could say another word.



Julian stared at the phone, stunned by what had just happened.He barely managed to keep his composure."She actually hung up on me?"



Paula looked at him nervously. "Did you do something to upset her, Mr. Powell? Maybe you should do something special to make it up to Mrs. Powell."


Julian didn't answer right away, his features clouded as he tried to piece everything together.


His thoughts drifted back to that night Yvonne begged him to stay when Rita's discomfort drove him to visit her. Explaining something so minor never appealed to him,yet if Yvonne kept pressing, it would only shatter the calm he enjoyed now.



Now that Rodger was finally getting better, the last thing Julian wanted was to let his grandfather stress over things between him and Yvonne.



"You should really talk to her, Mr. Powell. Most women just want to feel appreciated. A small surprise goes a long way." From the side, Paula tried to encourage him.



That suggestion sparked a memory. Yvonne had recently posted a picture of a puppy on Instagram,gushing about how adorable it was. She clearly loved little animals.



Hiding any hint of his frustration, Julian reached for his phone and called his assistant, Morton Perry. His voice was firm. "Track down Yvonne's location."



He paused for a moment, then cleared his throat before saying, "There's an auction coming up in a few days. A purebred poodle's on the list. I want you to win it for me."



Morton responded right away, "Understood, sir."


A surge of irritation washed over Julian as he ended the call. An uneasy sensation settled in as he took a slow look around the empty villa.


A question nagged at him-for the past three years,had Yvonne been waiting alone in this cold house for him to come home from work every day?


Usually, Julian didn't dwell on the past, but today,every corner seemed to whisper her name.


He wandered into the bedroom, where the perfectly made bed greeted him. His expression grew darker.


Memories surfaced, he and Yvonne had once shared their first intimacy on that very bed, just like any married couple would.


The more he dwelled on the details of that night, the more restless he felt, A dry, uneasy feeling crept over him, and he headed straight for a cold shower.


When morning broke, Julian woke at six, heading to the home gym as usual.



Finishing a round of exercises, he glanced at the empty spot beside him. He remembered the days when Yvonne would linger there, watching him with adoring eyes while he worked out at home.



That emptiness left him unsettled long before the day had even started.


After wiping the sweat from his brow, he walked out  of the gym and into the dining room, where a plate of plain toast and a glass of milk waited on the table.


Yvonne always went out of her way to cook a bowl of warm porridge for him, knowing how sensitive his stomach was. She'd serve it with fresh, light side dishes, nothing like the bland breakfast the staff had set out today.


A rush of frustration made his fists clench, his stare icy.


Ignoring the meal, he grabbed his phone and used a different number to text Yvonne. "Come home, let's talk things over."


This time, his message didn't get blocked.


Then, thinking he sounded too harsh, he worried Yvonne might dig in her heels even more. He followed up with a softer note. "I bought a puppy for you. It's adorable. Come see it."



That message bounced back, she'd blocked this number as well.



He sat there, lost for words.



Just then, Paula walked in with a stack of packages and set an envelope on the table.


She glanced his way. "You have a letter, Mr. Powell.Looks urgent, seems to be from Mrs. Powell." The icy mask Julian wore faded for a split second, and a small,self-satisfied smile tugged at his lips. He tried to act like it didn't matter, but he tore the letter open the moment Paula dropped it.



However, when he got a full understanding of the content, his smile vanished at once.
Inside the envelope was a divorce agreement.
###Chapter 12 Found Someone Else

Julian's expression turned to stone as he stared down at the divorce papers. Without a word, he let out a dry laugh, snatched up the agreement, and tore it into pieces.


The shredded paper drifted to the floor, scattering everywhere.



Paula, standing off to the side, was visibly nervous.She kept her eyes on the floor, hoping not to draw any attention.


Despite the tension in the air, Julian's next question came out steady. "Where was this letter sent from?"



Paula faltered, and her voice trembled, "I,I don't know."



Julian massaged his temples, realizing Yvonne would never make it easy for him to track her down if she was determined to keep her distance.


In his mind, she'd gone overboard this time. Clearly,she wanted to make a scene, probably to get Rodger involved and take her side.



Julían felt no guilt over his actions. To him, Yvonne  was simply blowing things out of proportion.


A sudden bark cut through the tension. Looking toward the door, Julian saw Morton arrive, holding a small puppy in his arms.



The puppy's irresistible charm drew a rare softness from Morton, and his usual sternness faded as he cradled it with a faint, gentle smile.



Julian's mood, however, only worsened at the sight.The puppy was meant for Yvonne, and now the gesture felt hollow.



Before Morton could come in fully, Julian waved him off. "Forget it. Take the dog with you. I don't want it anymore."



Morton froze in disbelief."What?"



After years of working for Julian, he still couldn't predict his boss's sudden changes in mood.


Julian had been thrilled about getting the puppy just yesterday, yet now he didn't want it at all. Had he gotten into a fight with Yvonne?


Morton shot a glance at Paula, who gave a tiny nod.in response. The two exchanged a silent understanding.



Julían paid no mind to their quiet signals. His attention remained on the envelope, his mood growing darker  by the second. His tone was harsh as he barked out an order. "I want Yvonne's location in one hour. No excuses."







At Kumvine Hospital, Yvonne and Spencer had just walked out to the front entrance. While making their way down the steps, she slipped and twisted her ankle,prompting Spencer to catch her at once, worry written all over his face.



He immediately asked, "Did you hurt yourself?"



Yvonne pulled back gently, offering him a reassuring smile. "I'm alright. Thank you for everything these past few days. You can go back to work now, I'll manage."



Spencer flashed a lazy grin. "My schedule's clear. Let me see you home.I insist."



In reality, Spencer should have been preparing for an important medical conference in Soblon. His original flight was set for this afternoon, but just earlier, he pushed it back to another day.



He'd let his chance with Yvonne slip away three years ago, convinced there wouldn't be another. But now that he knew she didn't have a happy marriage,he refused to sit back and let the same regret consume him twice. Noticing Yvonne's hesitation, Spencer gave the bag in his hand a little shake. "These are your prenatal supplements. I can go over the instructions with you."


That left Yvonne with no good reason to turn him down, so she agreed. The moment she nodded,Spencer's face lit up and he set off with enthusiasm.



He pointed toward his car with a spark of excitement."It's right over there. Come on, let's go!"



Yvonne fell into step behind Spencer. Their friendship went back years, and as he kept the conversation lively, she couldn't help but let out a genuine laugh.


Unbeknownst to her, Julian was watching from a distance in his car.



The moment Julian had found out Yvonne was at the hospital, he had sped over without wasting a second.


He had arrived just in time to catch sight of Yvonne smiling and chatting freely with another man.



It struck him that he couldn't remember the last time she had looked at him with that kind of lively smile.



Julian's glare grew frosty as he watched her, a humorless laugh escaping him. A surge of anger roiled inside him. She'd really crossed a line this time, ignoring his messages, blocking his calls, vanishing from his life,and then sending him divorce papers. Was this all because she had found someone else? He'd never been treated like this by anyone, let alone humiliated in such a way.



His gaze locked onto Spencer's car as it slowly reversed out of its parking space.



Without warning, Julian floored the accelerator and shot straight toward Spencer's car.
###Chapter 13 Suffocating Possessiveness
Spencer eased the car out of the parking space,trading lighthearted chatter with Yvonne. But their laughter cut short when a sleek black luxury car shot toward them out of nowhere.



Startled, Spencer slammed on the brakes. The tires screeched, the car whipping in a half-spin before jerking to a halt-barely two feet from disaster.



Heart pounding, Spencer twisted toward Yvonne at once. "Yvonne,are you hurt?"



She clutched the seatbelt as if it were a lifeline, her knuckles white, her face drained of color. She only managed a small shake of her head, eyes wide with fear.



Fury tightening his jaw, Spencer tore at his seatbelt buckle, ready to storm out and confront the reckless driver.



Just then, the black car's headlights blinked in a deliberate rhythm-taunting, like a predator flashing its fangs.



Yvonne lifted a trembling hand to shield her eyes from the glare, peering through her fingers until the license plate came into focus. Her stomach lurched-Julian's car.



Almost immediately, her phone buzzed in her palm.The number flashing on the screen was unfamiliar,yet she knew without doubt it was Julian calling.



Her face darkened as she hesitated, then reluctantly swiped to answer.



Julian's voice cut through the line, cold and commanding, brooking no argument."Get out."


Her breath caught in her throat, defiance rising to her lips, but before she could speak, the call clicked off,leaving only the dead tone ringing in her ears.



Almost instantly, the car facing them blasted its horn,a sharp command for her to act.



Yvonne's teeth sank into her lip before she finally pushed the door open. Her hand barely touched the handle when Spencer caught it, his grip firm,his head shaking in protest.



His eyes burned as he stared at her. "Yvonne, don't do this."



He wasn't blind; the situation was clear enough. His glare cut toward Julian's car, simmering with hostility "No one has the right to force you into anything You're already divorcing him-there's no reason to let yourself be trapped again," Spencer said, his voice steady and resolute.



From inside the luxury car, Julian narrowed his eyes,locking onto Spencer in a cold, wordless standoff.He then set his eyes on their clasped hands, and a shadow passed over his face, his jaw tightening with unspoken fury.



The razor-sharp intensity of his stare made Yvonne's spine prickle. She snatched her hand away from Spencer's, her pulse quickening.



She knew Julian's temperament better than anyone -his possessiveness was a cage lined with knives. If she dared stay inside Spencer's car,he would surely drag Spencer into his storm.



"Don't worry about me," Yvonne murmured, forcing a fragile smile that didn't reach her eyes. She unlatched the door and stepped out, her movements heavy with reluctance as she walked toward Julian's car,waiting like a predator in the dark.



Inside, Julian reclined against the leather seat with ease, one hand drumming an idle rhythm on the steering wheel. His eyes tracked her approach,and the faint curve of satisfaction at his lips hinted at a victory only he recognized. 
Like a monarch who believed the world bent to his will,he radiated certainty that she wouldn't dare defy him.



Yvonne drew in a steadying breath, hating the domineering air that clung to Julian. To her,his sudden appearance had nothing to do with care or concern-only the flare of his suffocating possessiveness.



She had dared to break free, to file for divorce, and he clearly saw that act as nothing less than a direct challenge to his authority.



Her expression remained frosty as she settled into the passenger seat, buckling her seatbelt in silence,not sparing himn a word.



Julian's gaze lingered on her cold detachment,and the memory of that divorce agreement ignited a fresh wave of fury.


His lips curled into a mocking sneer. "So,you're really leaving me for him, is that it? You really do have terrible taste in men."



Julian's lips curved in a faint sneer. He knew exactly who Spencer was-the heir of Briggs Pharmaceutical Corporation. The Briggs family was wealthy, but in his eyes,still leagues below the Powell family.


Yvonne's brows knit together. She parted her lips,  wanting to clarify that she and Spencer were nothing more than friends. But before she could utter a word,Julian's volatile temper snapped. The engine roared as he slammed his foot down on the accelerator.



The sudden lurch sent the car surging forward,wrenching a startled gasp from Yvonne. Her hand shot to the grab handle for balance, panic flashing in her eyes. "What on earth are you doing? Slow down!"



Julian's face stayed cold, unreadable, as his foot pressed mercilessly on the gas.
###Chapter 14 Twisted Satisfaction
Julian's car shot down the road, weaving between vehicles at breakneck speed. Yvonne gripped the grab handle with white knuckles, her face drained of all color.



Inside the car, silence stretched between them.Julian's fury simmered just beneath the surface, a storm he barely kept contained.



Despite the chaos on the road, he maneuvered with flawless control, slipping through traffic at reckless speeds and skimming past several near collisions.


After narrowly missing another car, Yvonne's restraint broke, and her voice shook as she pleaded, "Please,slow down."



But the wind rushing past the windows drowned her out completely.



Fear mingled wit hurt, and Yvonne's composure finally broke. Tears streamed down her face as she crumpled into the seat, feeling lost and defenseless.



The sight of her curled up and sobbing snapped Julian back to reality. The car screeched to a sudden stop as  he slammed on the brakes. He started to say something, but Yvonne was already brushing away her tears and firmly pushing the door open to get out.



A new wave of frustration surged through Julian. He rarely let his emotions get the better of him, yet today they kept slipping through his grasp. Without even realizing it, he had already seized Yvonne and pulled her back, pinning her against the seat.



"Is that it? You can't wait to run off and see your new man?" His voice was harsh.



Yvonne froze, her eyes wide in disbelief. Her anger flared, and she let out a cold laugh. "And what does it matter to you?"


Julian stared at her, caught off guard by the defiance in her voice. She felt like a stranger now. Gone was the softness in her gaze; only mockery remained.



Her voice was sharper than ever as she threw his words back at him. "Let's not forget, Julian, our marriage is just a front for Rodger's sake. If I have someone else, it's none of your concern!"



He remembered his own promise from before, the freedom he'd granted her as long as appearances were kept for Rodger's sake.


Now, hearing those words thrown in his face,a wave of displeasure washed over him. A chill settled in his  gaze as he clenched his lips in silence.


Watching him unravel like that, Yvonne's expression shifted ever so slightly, touched by a trace of satisfaction, as if his frustration gave her some twisted sense of pleasure.



She suddenly looped her arms around his neck,drawing close. Julian could feel her breath at his ear,his own breath catching as tension crackled in the small space between them.



But her next words were as cold as ice. "I'm done playing this game, Julian. I want adivorce."


Her closeness vanished as quickly as it came, leaving Julian reeling-he couldn't tell if it was from rage or something deeper. All he knew was that his self-control unraveled.



Without thinking, he caught her by the neck, dragging her back and crushing her lips with his in a rough,desperate kiss.


Watching her recoil in shock, wiping her lips with shaking hands, Julian felt a twisted satisfaction.



She glared. "Have you lost your mind?"


He absentmindedly touched his lips, surprised at how soft hers had been; how had he never noticed that before? As Yvonne bristled, Julian pulled himself together, his voice cool and steady. "You want to call it quits now?Let's not rewrite history. You cornered me into this marriage with Grandpa's help. And now..."

###Chapter 15 Kiss



Yvonne shook with fury, but when her gaze locked on Julian's eyes, the fire in her chest guttered out, leaving only a hollow ache. A broken laugh escaped her lips."Julian... I'm tired of this."



She lingered onhis face-the man she had clung to,loved fiercely for three long years. Her voice softened with regret. "I never should've forced you into this marriage. That was my mistake. I know now you don't love me, and I won't chain you anymore. Gofind your happiness. Just... let me go."

Her hands clenched, her eyes flashing. "Do you really not understand plain words?" Anger stirred beneath the grief in her chest, because no matter what, this man could always rattle her-whether it was joy or rage.

Yvonne had once tiptoed around Julian, careful not to breathe wrong in his presence. Her defiance,however, sent Julian's temper spiraling.

When the looming shadow fell across her, she instinctively shrank back to the other side. his arms, and strode forward without hesitation. "As long as we're not divorced, you're still my wife,"he growled, his voice low and unyielding. ###Chapter 16 End It



The weather in June shifted in an instant, rain hammering against the glass in a relentless rhythm while lightning tore through the sky and thunder shook the ground.

Gone was the fury that had consumed him moments earlier. Now his touch was calculated, patient, every movement designed to provoke, as if determined to prove she still wanted him.


Yvonne's joy shimmered faintly beneath her pain. No matter how deeply she had been wounded, her feelings for Julian burned stubbornly on, and even the faintest brush of his hand could awaken a dangerous longing inside her. When he finally let go of her wrists,she didn't even remember to fight back.



His lips captured hers, and his fingers wove tightly with her own, mirroring that night that had been seared into her memory.



The images overlapped-then versus now. Back then,their encounter had been reckless, rough, fueled by alcohol and desperation. Tonight, his touch carried an unfamiliar tenderness, so careful that her lashes fluttered closed, her defenses dissolving as she yielded to the heat of the moment.
