After navigating a maze of corridors, they reached a lavish private villa.


"Vince is hosting a big party here tonight," Andrew announced.



The party was in full swing-soft music floated through the air, a champagne fountain bubbled, and elegantly dressed guests mingled with polished smiles.



It seemed like a standard high-society affair, not particularly extravagant.



Yvonne grew more baffled by Andrew's intentions.Uninterested in the party's allure, Yvonne brushed off Andrew's presence and retreated to a quiet corner, nursing a drink while her eyes searched the crowd for Vince.



The room was filled with familiar faces-celebrities renowned for their charitable deeds and warmth, much like Vince, mingled with heirs of affluent families, some of whom Yvonne recognized from past events.


Yet, as she had never been introduced as Julian's wife in public, she remained a stranger to them.


As she observed, a vague unease gnawed at her.After a moment's reflection, she pinpointed its source.



The guests' smiles radiated a disturbing excitement,like addicts craving their next hit or predators eyeing vulnerable prey. Their fervor felt darkly unsettling.


Yvonne wondered if Andrew's vague insinuations were clouding her judgment. Then, she realized he had slipped away-he had been beside her moments ago, chatting with someone.



A quick glance around failed to locate him, so she shook it off, choosing not to fixate. Her sole aim tonight was to connect with Vince, and that was enough. Just then, a burst of fervent applause broke her thoughts. Turning toward the sound, she saw a man in a mink coat, cigar clenched in his mouth,being escorted to the villa's center by an adoring entourage.



He looked to be in his late thirties, his mature,striking features at odds with the ostentatious coat.Yet, his eager smile, matching the crowd's, twisted his demeanor from refined to menacingly eerie.



Yvonne stood frozen, stunned. This was nothing like the Vince she recalled from his on-screen persona.What had changed in his years away from the limelight?



Her stare must have been too intense, as Vince's gaze locked onto hers.



As the villa echoed with applause, every eye turned toward Yvonne.



She stepped back, a shiver running through her.


The scene felt ripped from a horror film. Then,Vince approached with a sly grin. "Are you the one Andrew brought along? His latest fling? Quite a catch."



His indifferent tone clashed sharply with the gracious actor Yvonne remembered, once lauded by the press as a paragon of respect toward women.


Swallowing her discomfort, Yvonne steadied herself and said, "Mr. Greville, I'm here to offer you the lead role in my film."
###Chapter 96 Imagination Collapsed





The villa hushed briefly before bursting into mocking laughter.


Vince, chuckling, clamped his cigar between his teeth, took a puff, and muttered through squinted eyes, "And you are? If Andrew had said this, I would have listened. But he just left."



Learning that Andrew had slipped away, Yvonne felt a mix of surprise and frustration, annoyed that Andrew would bring her to this strange place only to abandon her without a word.



But that was irrelevant now. Taking a steadying breath, she kept her cool. "This project is unrelated to Andrew. It is a Powell Group venture."


"Powell Group?" Vince's gaze sharpened briefly,but upon eyeing Yvonne, his expression shifted to scorn."You think I'm an idiot, young lady? The Powell Group sent a young girl like you to negotiate alone? I think you're just tossing their name around to scam your way in!"


"Mr. Greville, I'm telling the truth. You saw my script and said it intrigued you!" Yvonne pressed.


"Oh, that was your script.." Vince murmured, his tone soft.



A spark of hope flared in Yvonne's eyes, only to be snuffed out as he smirked. "I was just messing with you. I never even read your script."


Her optimism crumbled, leaving her stunned. How could this be?



Andrew's cryptic warnings echoed in her mind, and she realized seeing was indeed different from hearing.


The crowd watched her like she was a circus act.Vince exhaled a plume of cigar smoke, sneering,"Even if it's a Powell Group project, it's some tiny,irrelevant thing, right? I'm about to sign for their blockbuster. Why would I pick your little gig?" Yvonne clenched her jaw, her eyes blazing. "You haven't read my script, so you have no right to dismiss it! I believe my script is strong enough to win over anyone who cares about real cinema!"


"Oh, really? Now you've piqued my interest." Vince's eyes glinted with mockery, his lips curling in amusement.


Yvonne's heart lifted for a moment, but his next words cut through. "With such big talk, how much can you.offer me? And what's the budget for this little project of yours?"


The questions struck her where it hurt most, and Yvonne went quiet, words failing her.


The crowd's jeering laughter swelled, their skepticism about her ties to the Powell Group deepening. After all, the powerhouse Powell Group was known for its financial swagger, never hesitating to throw around its wealth.



The evening had been a relentless assault on Yvonne's assumptions, exposing her idealism as painfully naive. Still, she couldn't hold back. "You said you would work for free if the script was good enough...


"What, you think this is some fairy tale?" Vince cut her off, his tone dripping with scorn. "I'm not handing out freebies. You don't know how this business works,do you?"


The laughter around her grew louder, biting. Yvonne stood rooted, chewing her lip, feeling like the butt of a cruel joke.



Vince had closed the distance, now looming in front of her. He took a long pull from his cigar and exhaled a cloud of smoke directly into her face.


Then he said, "Tell you what, spend the night with me, and I'll do your film for nothing."


The foul stench of tobacco choked her, sparking a coughing fit. Rage surged, and she glared at him,her hand flying out to deliver a sharp slap across his face."In your dreams!" Julian always refrained from smoking around her, yet Vince had the audacity to puff smoke directly in her face, an insult she refused to endure.


Her fleeting triumph, however, ignited his fury.


"You've got some guts, hitting me on my own ground!" he snarled.


At his command, the crowd inched closer, their presence suffocating. Yvonne's fists tightened, and she spun toward the exit, adrenaline pumping.


This was an exclusive club, but as long as she left,she believed these high-profile figures wouldn't stoop to violence.


"Stop her!" Vince's voice was ice-cold.


A group of people rushed after her as she bolted for the door. Just as escape seemed within reach, a sickening thud echoed.


A bloodied figure plummeted from the second floor,crashing to the floor right in her path.
###Chapter 97 Lambs





The shocking scene froze Yvonne in place, her ears ringing as if the world had muffled into a distant hum,pierced by raucous cheers.


Slowly, she turned her rigid neck toward the spot where the figure had crashed.


On the villa's second floor, an impeccably dressed crowd gathered, their excitement palpable as someone uncorked a champagne bottle, fueling their wild applause.


Yvonne recoiled in horror, struck by their callousness.



(

How could they revel with such joy when a person seemed to have died before their eyes?


Abruptly, the supposedly lifeless figure sprawled on the ground convulsed in agony, jolting Yvonne with shock, though she quickly discerned the person was
still alive.


He labored to lift himself-it was a teenage boy, with slightly wavy, lengthy hair, potentially striking in appearance, though a gash on his forehead,oozing blood,masked his face.


The crimson stream trailed down his cheeks, staining his worn, threadbare garments, giving the deceptive impression of a ghastly, lethal wound that had tricked Yvonne.



"You..." Yvonne stammered, her throat tight with nerves, poised to ask about his state when raucous cheers exploded from the upper floor.


"Check that out! That bastard is tougher than he looks! He is still alive!"


"Mr. Greville, can the party begin now? Is this woman part of the wager?"


Yvonne's eyes narrowed as she stiffly turned to see Vince and his entourage emerging.


Vince's eyes glinted with a sly grin. "This is Andrew's woman. We owe him some courtesy."


The crowd groaned in disappointment.


"However..." Vince continued, sparking their curiosity with a wicked shrug. "This venue is vast, and I can't monitor every corner. With him absent, a little lapse is only natural, don't you think?"


The group roared in approval, their predatory gazes fixed on Yvonne, as if she were prey ripe for the taking.


A voice boomed from the balcony, "Ladies and gentlemen, let the games begin! The highest bidder can take the two lambs home tonight!"


Chaos erupted, leaving Yvonne disoriented. What bids? What did "take the two lambs home" mean?What sort of event was this?



Just then, she noticed the teenage boy beside her tense at the sight of Vince.


With a sudden burst, he lunged at Vince, growling like a vengeful wolf pup consumed by rage. "You monster! You will pay for my sister's death!"


The teenage boy barely got near before a wall of bodyguards halted him mid-stride.


Vince's mouth twisted into a mocking smile as he scoffed, "Kid, let's set the record straight. Your sister sold herself for money. She willingly became a prostitute. How can you pin that on me?"


The teenage boy's eyes blazed with fury, tears spilling uncontrollably as he wailed in anguish."Why?Why wasn't it enough to kill my sister? Why destroy me too? Don't the poor have a right to exist?"


"You're right, the poor have no place in this world!"The smug response came from the haughty guests surrounding them.


With a flick of Vince's hand, the bodyguards seized the teenage boy, dragging him towards the luxurious champagne waterfall.


In a flash, his head was plunged into the gushing liquid. His eyes bulged in panic as he thrashed violently to break free.


The elite guests watched with glee as his struggles weakened, as if death were imminent.


Yvonne's blood ran cold, memories of her own near-drowning in the swimming pool flooding back.


In that moment, a surge of bravery welled within her,and without a second thought, she charged forward,toppling the champagne structure.


Liquor flooded the ground, and the teenage boy gasped faintly, like a fish teetering on the edge of survival.
###Chapter 98 Threat





The heavy scent of spilled liquor dissipated, leaving a chilling tension in the air.


"Are you alright?" Yvonne inquired, seemingly unaware of the menacing stares fixed on her.Kneeling to assist the young man, her tone brimmed with worry.


The frail, disheveled teen shook his head, gazing up at her with eyes reflecting both bewilderment and dread-bewilderment that anyone would defend him in such a merciless place, and dread because the harsh truth loomed. They were like cornered prey amidst ravenous beasts, just him and her, who seemed ill-equipped for a fight.


To him, escape felt like a distant dream, and her presence only meant another soul doomed to his grim fate.


Barely stepping into adulthood, the teenage boy's courage wavered, tears streaming down his face.


Yvonne, at a loss for how to console him, paused in silence before facing Vince.


"What's the cost to free him?" she demanded.



By now, she knew reasoning with these callous elites was futile; they only valued gain.


At her words, Vince's eyes narrowed, and with a subtle gesture, a bodyguard beside him hesitantly extended a hand.


Vince pressed his lit cigar into the guard's palm,snuffing it out. The guard's face glistened with sweat from the agony, yet he stayed silent.


To these affluent elites, the poor were mere playthings.


Vince's voice was icy. "No amount will free him now.You might even lose yourself here."


With that, a wave of bodyguards advanced.


While Vince might hesitate to defy Andrew alone, this gathering was a sacred tradition among the elite.Since Yvonne, brought by Andrew, had broken their unspoken code, they deemed her accountable.


The trembling teen gripped Yvonne's hand,pleading,"Miss, abandon me and escape. These people are monsters!"



Yvonne gently tousled his hair, then faced the crowd,drawing her phone. Its screen showed a recording in progress.



With unwavering resolve, she declared, "I've captured everything that just happened. None of you wants this online, do you?"


Pandemonium erupted in the space. Most attendees were high-profile figures, celebrities like Vince.


Yvonne locked eyes with one and said, "Robin Hardy,you just signed with a luxury brand, didn't you? A scandal now-imagine the contract penalties ruining your career."


Upstairs, the named celebrity turned pale instantly. She then turned to another. "Adrian Morphew, a world-famous philanthropist, what a shock to find you here..."



A mustached older man looked panicked.



Yvonne steadily named others, each mention stoking their panic.



Smiling calmly, she added, "I assure you, every face in this video is unmistakable, leaving no room for denial."



The crowd's alarm morphed into rage, many directing their fury at Vince.



"Vince, fix this! You hosted this event-if that video leaks, you're finished too!"


Vince's expression darkened as he glared at Yvonne,then flashed his trademark charming grin. "Let's see if you can leave this place."


He raised a hand with a casual wave. "Seize that phone!" A horde of bodyguards surged toward Yvonne and the teen. Grabbing the boy, Yvonne spun to flee but tripped, her ankle twisting as she fell.


The guards surrounded them. Vince approached with a sinister smirk. "You bitch, I'll make you regret this!"His hand rose to strike.



At that instant, a commanding voice boomed. "I dare anyone to lay a finger on her!"


All eyes turned as the villa's main gate burst open,a man striding in, flanked by his own bodyguards.
###Chapter 99 Blacklisted





Julian entered with confidence, clad in a custom-fitted suit that highlighted his imposing, statuesque frame.His gleaming dress shoes clicked purposefully against the floor with each step.


The moment he entered, a hush fell over the sprawling mansion. Not a soul stirred or uttered a word.


All attention locked onto Julian as he moved toward Yvonne, bending slightly to pull her into a warm embrace.



His fingers gently combed through her tangled locks,untidy from her desperate attempt to flee, his face radiating affection.


Beneath his composed demeanor, however, Yvonne detected a chilling fury. This anger wasn't aimed at her but at Andrew, who had just slunk back, his face bruised as though struck, his spirit utterly deflated. "Next time you want to go somewhere, just let me know, and I'll take you. Don't sneak off with someone else, alright?" Julian murmured to Yvonne.


Andrew, realizing his error, stammered an explanation, but Julian's sharp, unyielding stare left him trembling, forcing him to bow his head in defeat.


Throughout the exchange, Julian didn't so much as glance at Vince, who stood before him.


The room was filled with prominent, high-profile figures, yet Julian's presence reduced them to silence, their breaths shallow with fear.


Despite Vince's own prestige and accomplishments,Julian's aura made him feel like an insignificant speck, unnoticed and irrelevant.


Caught between dread and resentment, Vince mustered the courage to speak. "Mr. Powell, l..."


Before he could finish, Julian's cold, commanding gaze silenced him, leaving him frozen, as if the air had been sucked from his lungs. He stood paralyzed, cursing his luck internally.


His thoughts spiraled in disbelief-why was Julian here, at an event he would typically deem beneath him?



A realization hit Vince, and he shot a wary glance at Yvonne, suspecting she hadn't exaggerated her ties to the Powell Group, perhaps even sharing a unique bond with Julian.



As Julian stepped closer, Vince, despite their similar stature, felt diminished, shrinking under his presence.



"Did you plan to hurt my woman?" Julian's tone was glacial.


Vince collapsed to his knees with a heavy thud, tears streaming as he begged, "It was a misunderstanding,Mr. Powell! I had no idea she was yours! I wouId have shown her nothing but respect if I had known!"


Seeing Julian unmoved, Vince scrambled toward Yvonne, pleading desperately, "Please,tell Mr.Powell we're friends, that it was all in jest, alright? You wanted me for your movie, didn't you? I'll do it without a fee!"



Yvonne's view of Vince soured further; his sudden opportunism was repulsive. Recalling the ordeal, a wave of revulsion hit her, and she spat with contempt, "I would never cast someone like you in my film!" Had Julian not arrived when he did, her fate could have been dire.


With an icy glare and no trace of doubt, Yvonne turned to Julian. "I don't know him, and we're definitely not friends. Do what you need to."


Vince's panic surged, his frantic apologies accompanied by tears. "Mr. Powell, please, don't kill me! I know I messed up!"
(

Julian's eyes narrowed, taking in Yvonne's disarrayed hair and tear-streaked face, clear signs of her distress.



His gaze grew frostier as it landed on Vince, his voice cutting like ice. "No need for such drama. We live in a civilized world, so naturally, I won't kill you."


Just as Vince began to exhale, a group of impeccably dressed figures strode through the entrance, exuding wealth and authority.


The mansion fell silent again, the gathered celebrities shrinking back, some lowering their gazes, others trying to blend into the shadowS.



These new arrivals were titans of the entertainment world, second only to Julian. Crossing any of them meant career suicide.



Unfortunately for these celebrities, those new arrivals were Julian's business allies, all eager to curry favour with the Powell Group.


Approaching Julian, they asked with concern,"What's going on, Mr. Powell?"


Julian glanced at Vince, who quivered like a frightened animal, on the verge of collapse, and gave a faint, chilling laugh. "Nothing serious. I've just learned Vince has no interest in the opportunities provided to him. Let's ensure he won't be bothered with such things anymore."


The message was unmistakable-Vince's career was over; he was effectively blacklisted from the entertainment industry.
###Chapter 100 Tenderness





Julian's threat to blacklist Vince from the industry was no mere warning-it was a devastating blow.


Vince knew this meant not only the entertainment world but every other sector would turn its back on him. It was a calculated move to strip him of all prospects, leaving him no place to stay in Kumvine.


Overwhelmed with dread, Vince scrambled toward Julian, his mind racing until he seized on a faint hope."Mr. Powell, I'm tied to Warren Pictures. You and Mr.Pearson are close, aren't you? For his sake, please..."


However, invoking Andrew was a grave mistake.Julian's face darkened instantly, a cold, mocking chuckle escaping his lips.


Andrew, who had been treading carefully, lurched forward, tripping in his haste, and delivered a furious kick to Vince's chest, his voice thick with righteous anger. "Shut up with your lies! Warren Pictures has already terminated your contract!"



The swelling on Andrew's face slurred his words slightly, and Yvonne, who had been frustrated with him, couldn't suppress a flicker of amusement.


Julian was likely the one who had left that mark on Andrew, wasn't he? Only Julian would dare to do such a thing, after all. Yvonne was certain of it.


After berating Vince, Andrew turned to Yvonne with a fawning smile. "Yvonne, do you think this punishment is sufficient?"



Caught off guard, Yvonne nodded absently, at a loss for words. Julian let out a sharp, dismissive huff, took her hand, and led her toward the exit.


At the club's entrance, a sleek luxury car idled.Julian's grip on Yvonne's wrist was firm as they approached, but she wriggled free, murmuring,"You're hurting me."



His jaw tightened, pent-up emotions boiling over as he faced her with a stern look. "Do you have any idea what kind of place this is? How could you come here?"



Yvonne's mind flashed to the chaotic scenes inside the villa-the raucous cheers, the bloodied teenage boy crumpled on the floor. Her face paled, fear creeping in, but she refused to back down in front of Julian,jutting out her chin. "Well, you're here too."


Her defiance caught him off guard, leaving him momentarily speechless. He reached into his pocket,pulling out a pack of cigarettes to steady his nerves.


Before he could light one, Yvonne's sharp voice cut through. "No smoking!"


The sight of cigarettes brought back the memory of Vince exhaling smoke in her face, filling her with revulsion.



Julian, who rarely smoked and never in Yvonne's presence, had only grabbed the pack in his agitation,craving the calm nicotine might offer.


At her command, he slipped it back into his pocket, exhaling heavily as he looked at her. "This club is notorious for its wild, shady dealings. It is backed by powerful people, operates on the edge of the law,and is full of dangerous chaos. You walked into this blind-it's not safe."



Julian couldn't help but feel a wave of relief that he had come here to discuss a project tonight and spotted Andrew at the entrance. That was how he learned Andrew had brought Yvonne here and then abandoned her.


Now, he regretted not landing another punch to even out Andrew's swollen face.



Hearing Julian's gentler tone, Yvonne felt a sudden rush of vulnerability. The fear she had suppressed surfaced, her voice quivering. "I get it now. Vince...he's nothing like his public persona..."



Her words faltered, choked by emotion. Julian drew her into his arms, his hand softly patting her shoulder. Unable to hold back, Yvonne's tears spilled over, her quiet sobs shaking her frame. She had been terrified, her hands trembling as she had brandished that video to fend off her attackers.Without Julian's arrival, she didn't know how she would have survived.


Clinging to him, Yvonne let her tears flow freely.


Beneath the soft night sky, Julian gently smoothed her hair, his gaze brimming with unspoken tenderness.
